              SELECT [u0].[Id], [u0].[FullName], [u0].[IsActive], [u0].[RoleId]
              FROM [Users] AS [u0]
              WHERE [u0].[IsActive] = CAST(1 AS bit)
          ) AS [t2] ON [a1].[UserId] = [t2].[Id]

              FROM [Roles] AS [r]
              WHERE [r].[IsActive] = CAST(1 AS bit)
          ) AS [t3] ON [t2].[RoleId] = [t3].[Id]
          WHERE [t2].[IsActive] = CAST(1 AS bit)
      ) AS [t1] ON [t].[Id] = [t1].[ApplicationId]
      ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t1].[Id0], [t1].[Id1]
